These nerves allow trunk motion and abdominal wall compression.</div><div style="color: rgb(100, 116, 139); margin-top: 8px; font-size: 14px;">Clinical Application: A massage therapist targeting abdominal breathing or tension may stimulate these nerves for relaxation.</div><div style="color: rgb(161, 98, 7); margin-top: 8px; font-size: 13px;">Source: Clinical Anatomy ‚Äì Snell</div><div style="color: rgb(100, 116, 139); margin-top: 8px; font-size: 13px;"><span>Tags: thoracoabdominal, abdominal wall, external oblique </span><span>Keywords: nerve supply, trunk movement, T12</span></div><div class="quiz-actions" role="group" aria-label="Quiz navigation actions"><button disabled="" aria-label="Previous question" role="button" aria-disabled="true">Previous</button><button disabled="" aria-label="Next question" role="button" aria-disabled="true" tabindex="0" data-testid="quiz-next-btn" style="visibility: visible;">Next</button><button aria-label="Finish quiz early" role="button" disabled="" aria-disabled="true">Finish</button></div></div></main></main><footer class="app-footer"><input class="question-search-bar" placeholder="Search questions..." aria-label="Search questions" type="text"></footer></div>
